<Text>Would totally recommend this place. I lived in Japan for 7 years or so and was so happy to find this place because the food actually tasted Japanese. There is so many restaurants that claim to be Japanese but they don‚Äôt even come close to tasting legit like in Japan. The moment I tasted their miso soup I just knew this place would be really good. So some other things I like about this place, the presentation of the place reminds of a Ramen shop I went to in Nagasaki and really brought up lots of memory lol. The place is well kept and clean. The staff was outstanding when it came to making sure we were taken care of and was very knowledgeable about dishes we didn‚Äôt know. The only complaint I have is the bathroom needs a renovation. < review>
My favourite out of the 3 done by the same owner. There's a long wait outside best to go very early or later or be prepared to shop around while you wait. The signup sheet is at the front. Tip if you're going with another person, one should get extra pork and share it  you can also ask for hot water to dilute the soup when you're almost done.< /review>

I've lived in and around Japan for an accumulation of 5 years. I can say this is the closest to authentic you're going to get out of this area of San Diego. The staff is friendly and the prices are reasonable. If you're looking for a place to have a bowl of Ramen and some drinks, I would hands down recommended this place!<//review>

The urgent care didnt call me till Sunday. So go to the labs website,  you will find out your results faster. Owner Harris is very nice and his providers were great!  Thank you AFC Ladera!</text>

< Text>
Doctors are nice, staff is kind of disorganized. Generally not the best experience.  This review spans my last two appointments, on 10/14/20 and today 4/12/21.

10/14/20: understanding that everyone was trying to adapt to COVID, my appointment was still rescheduled like 3 times. I finally had to explain the I'd be out of town from November through January, and refused to reschedule again. When I went in, despite having an appointment, I waited over an hour to be seen. All told, I probably spent 3hrs there that day, and by the time I left I was so hungry I couldn't think of anything else. The front desk was nice enough to give me a gift card for $100 and I went on my way.

4/12/21: Today I go in, and thankfully they've figured out their COVID protocol. I arrived 10 min early and I'm seen right on time. Cleaning and exam go well, but I'd also asked for a custom mouth guard which requires taking molds of my teeth. First they put the goop directly on my teeth, no tray. Then they took molds of top and bottom but didn't apply the tray correctly. So another technician takes over and takes 2 more molds of my top teeth (1 didn't set quite right), and 1 more of the bottom. Definitely didn't have to be as uncomfortable as all that, but happy to have accurate molds.

When I go to pay, come to find out that the gift card was only good for 90 days. The receptionist points at some fine print on the back of the card at the very bottom, and informs me that they haven't given gift cards out "in a very long time"...Okayyy 1. My appointments were almost exactly 6 months apart, standard for dental cleanings. 2. Since when do gift cards expire? 3. Who is going anywhere to lay with their mouth open every 90 days during COVID?! I said as much out loud, and the receptionist was nice enough to honor the gift card "as a gift" (again, huh??) because I'm moving in a few months.

You know, I've been a patient here for 2 years. Nothing really terrible has happened during that time, it's just been consistently ok. But the experience could definitely be improved</Text>

< Text>
This was my second visit to Karen Allen Salon in Temecula for color services.  Also my second time seeing Gentry, who is fantastic!  I highly recommend her for color.  Gentry is professional, sweet, fun to talk to, and technically very good.  She knows color, and she also listens and pays attention to details.  She doesn't try to upsell but does make me aware of products and services that I might be interested in.  She recommended adding on a gloss service with color (in addition to my touch-up) to spruce up my existing color, which I did and it really transformed my dull, dry hair.  I now have the glowing, shiny locks we all long for.  I look and feel beautiful after seeing Gentry, and feel like I've spent a couple of hours with a fun friend in a beautiful space.  The prices are reasonable and on-point for the level of service (and with promos--like first-time discounts and 2nd visit discounts, prices are even better).  Front staff have always been friendly and helpful.  And the space is light, bright, and lovely.  Love this salon, love Aveda color, and love Gentry!</Text>

<user_name>Celina Castro-Morgutia< /user_name><Date>1553975555368< /Date><Rate>3< /Rate>< Text>
Recently visited this office after the Chula Vista location messed things up. Thankfully, this location was able to take me in the next day. I went in to get all four of my wisdom teeth extracted. What they don't tell you is that the oral surgeon only comes once a month. Even though you have an appointment, you should expect to wait for more than 2-3 hours to see the surgeon. After waiting for almost 3 hours, I was finally seen by the surgeon to get my wisdom teeth taken out. I understand that the staff is frustrated by the amount of inquiries from all of the other patients regarding seeing the oral surgeon. I inquired about wait times more than two times and most of the front desk staff kept their demeanor cool and professional. However, there was one front desk employee who gave off an attitude when I asked why certain information wasn't given prior. Once I was sedated, it only took him about 40min to get all of my wisdom teeth out. I was thankful for a speedy procedure and the sedation completely knocks you out so I didn't feel a thing during. What I didn't like was that nobody went over what to expect or do after the extraction. What they sent me and my driver away with was a sheet telling us what to do. It would have been extremely helpful if someone went over this information with me before sedating me because I was left to google a lot of information on how to take care of myself / do's and don't after wisdom teeth removal. I am interested in getting braces through Western Dental but now I'm not so sure after my experience with them at their Chula Vista and National City location.<//Text>
